This pass modifies 'vectorizable' loops\\n10: // and generates target-independent LLVM-IR.\\n11: // The vectorizer uses the TargetTransformInfo analysis to estimate the costs\\n12: // of instructions in order to estimate the profitability of vectorization.\\n13: //\\n14: // The loop vectorizer combines consecutive loop iterations into a single\\n15: // 'wide' iteration. After this transformation the index is incremented\\n16: // by the SIMD vector width, and not by one.\\n17: //\\n18: // This pass has four parts:\\n19: // 1. The main loop pass that drives the different parts.\\n20: // 2. LoopVectorizationLegality - A unit that checks for the legality\\n21: //    of the vectorization.\\n22: // 3. InnerLoopVectorizer - A unit that performs the actual\\n23: //    widening of instructions.\\n24: // 4. LoopVectorizationCostModel - A unit that checks for the profitability\\n25: //    of vectorization. It decides on the optimal vector width, which\\n26: //    can be one, if vectorization is not profitable.\\n27: //\\n28: // There is a development effort going on to migrate loop vectorizer to the\\n29: // VPlan infrastructure and to introduce outer loop vectorization support (see\\n30: // docs/VectorizationPlan.rst and\\n31: // http://lists.llvm.org/pipermail/llvm-dev/2017-December/119523.html). For this\\n32: // purpose, we temporarily introduced the VPlan-native vectorization path: an\\n33: // alternative vectorization path that is natively implemented on top of the\\n34: // VPlan infrastructure. See EnableVPlanNativePath for enabling.\\n35: //\\n36: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n37: //\\n38: // The reduction-variable vectorization is based on the paper:\\n39: //  D. Nuzman and R. Henderson. Multi-platform Auto-vectorization.\\n40: //\\n41: // Variable uniformity checks are inspired by:\\n42: //  Karrenberg, R. and Hack, S. Whole Function Vectorization.\\n43: //\\n44: // The interleaved access vectorization is based on the paper:\\n45: //  Dorit Nuzman, Ira Rosen and Ayal Zaks.  Auto-Vectorization of Interleaved\\n46: //  Data for SIMD\\n47: //\\n48: // Other ideas/concepts are from:\\n49: //  A. Zaks and D. Nuzman. Autovectorization in GCC-two years later.\\n50: //\\n51: //  S. Maleki, Y. Gao, M. Garzaran, T. Wong and D. Padua.  An Evaluation of\\n52: //  Vectorizing Compilers.\\n53: //\\n54: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n55: \\n56: #ifndef LLVM_TRANSFORMS_VECTORIZE_LOOPVECTORIZE_H\\n57: #define LLVM_TRANSFORMS_VECTORIZE_LOOPVECTORIZE_H\\n58: \\n59: #include \\\"llvm/IR/PassManager.h\\\"\\n60: #include \\\"llvm/Support/CommandLine.h\\\"\\n61: #include \\\"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\\\"\\n62: #include \\\"llvm/Transforms/Utils/ExtraPassManager.h\\\"\\n63: #include <functional>\\n64: \\n65: namespace llvm {\\n66: \\n67: class AssumptionCache;\\n68: class BlockFrequencyInfo;\\n69: class DemandedBits;\\n70: class DominatorTree;\\n71: class Function;\\n72: class Instruction;\\n73: class Loop;\\n74: class LoopAccessInfoManager;\\n75: class LoopInfo;\\n76: class OptimizationRemarkEmitter;\\n77: class ProfileSummaryInfo;\\n78: class ScalarEvolution;\\n79: class TargetLibraryInfo;\\n80: class TargetTransformInfo;\\n81: \\n82: LLVM_ABI extern cl::opt<bool> EnableLoopInterleaving;\\n83: LLVM_ABI extern cl::opt<bool> EnableLoopVectorization;\\n84: \\n85: struct LoopVectorizeOptions {\\n86:   /// If false, consider all loops for interleaving.\\n87:   /// If true, only loops that explicitly request interleaving are considered.\\n88:   bool InterleaveOnlyWhenForced;\\n89: \\n90:   /// If false, consider all loops for vectorization.\\n91:   /// If true, only loops that explicitly request vectorization are considered.\\n92:   bool VectorizeOnlyWhenForced;\\n93: \\n94:   /// The current defaults when creating the pass with no arguments are:\\n95:   /// EnableLoopInterleaving = true and EnableLoopVectorization = true. This\\n96:   /// means that interleaving default is consistent with the cl::opt flag, while\\n97:   /// vectorization is not.\\n98:   /// FIXME: The default for EnableLoopVectorization in the cl::opt should be\\n99:   /// set to true, and the corresponding change to account for this be made in\\n100:   /// opt.cpp. The initializations below will become:\\n101:   /// InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(!EnableLoopInterleaving)\\n102:   /// VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(!EnableLoopVectorization).\\n103:   LoopVectorizeOptions()\\n104:       : InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(false), VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(false) {}\\n105:   LoopVectorizeOptions(bool InterleaveOnlyWhenForced,\\n106:                        bool VectorizeOnlyWhenForced)\\n107:       : InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(InterleaveOnlyWhenForced),\\n108:         VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(VectorizeOnlyWhenForced) {}\\n109: \\n110:   LoopVectorizeOptions &setInterleaveOnlyWhenForced(bool Value) {\\n111:     InterleaveOnlyWhenForced = Value;\\n112:     return *this;\\n113:   }\\n114: \\n115:   LoopVectorizeOptions &setVectorizeOnlyWhenForced(bool Value) {\\n116:     VectorizeOnlyWhenForced = Value;\\n117:     return *this;\\n118:   }\\n119: };\\n120: \\n121: /// Storage for information about made changes.\\n122: struct LoopVectorizeResult {\\n123:   bool MadeAnyChange;\\n124:   bool MadeCFGChange;\\n125: \\n126:   LoopVectorizeResult(bool MadeAnyChange, bool MadeCFGChange)\\n127:       : MadeAnyChange(MadeAnyChange), MadeCFGChange(MadeCFGChange) {}\\n128: };\\n129: \\n130: /// The LoopVectorize Pass.\\n131: struct LoopVectorizePass : public PassInfoMixin<LoopVectorizePass> {\\n132: private:\\n133:   /// If false, consider all loops for interleaving.\\n134:   /// If true, //===- LoopVectorize.h ------------------------------------------*- C++ -*-===//\\n2: //\\n3: // Part of the LLVM Project, under the Apache License v2.0 with LLVM Exceptions.\\n4: // See https://llvm.org/LICENSE.txt for license information.\\n5: // SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 WITH LLVM-exception\\n6: //\\n7: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n8: //\\n9: // This is the LLVM loop vectorizer. This pass modifies 'vectorizable' loops\\n10: // and generates target-independent LLVM-IR.\\n11: // The vectorizer uses the TargetTransformInfo analysis to estimate the costs\\n12: // of instructions in order to estimate the profitability of vectorization.\\n13: //\\n14: // The loop vectorizer combines consecutive loop iterations into a single\\n15: // 'wide' iteration. After this transformation the index is incremented\\n16: // by the SIMD vector width, and not by one.\\n17: //\\n18: // This pass has four parts:\\n19: // 1. The main loop pass that drives the different parts.\\n20: // 2. LoopVectorizationLegality - A unit that checks for the legality\\n21: //    of the vectorization.\\n22: // 3. InnerLoopVectorizer - A unit that performs the actual\\n23: //    widening of instructions.\\n24: // 4. LoopVectorizationCostModel - A unit that checks for the profitability\\n25: //    of vectorization. It decides on the optimal vector width, which\\n26: //    can be one, if vectorization is not profitable.\\n27: //\\n28: // There is a development effort going on to migrate loop vectorizer to the\\n29: // VPlan infrastructure and to introduce outer loop vectorization support (see\\n30: // docs/VectorizationPlan.rst and\\n31: // http://lists.llvm.org/pipermail/llvm-dev/2017-December/119523.html). For this\\n32: // purpose, we temporarily introduced the VPlan-native vectorization path: an\\n33: // alternative vectorization path that is natively implemented on top of the\\n34: // VPlan infrastructure. See EnableVPlanNativePath for enabling.\\n35: //\\n36: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n37: //\\n38: // The reduction-variable vectorization is based on the paper:\\n39: //  D. Nuzman and R. Henderson. Multi-platform Auto-vectorization.\\n40: //\\n41: // Variable uniformity checks are inspired by:\\n42: //  Karrenberg, R. and Hack, S. Whole Function Vectorization.\\n43: //\\n44: // The interleaved access vectorization is based on the paper:\\n45: //  Dorit Nuzman, Ira Rosen and Ayal Zaks.  Auto-Vectorization of Interleaved\\n46: //  Data for SIMD\\n47: //\\n48: // Other ideas/concepts are from:\\n49: //  A. Zaks and D. Nuzman. Autovectorization in GCC-two years later.\\n50: //\\n51: //  S. Maleki, Y. Gao, M. Garzaran, T. Wong and D. Padua.  An Evaluation of\\n52: //  Vectorizing Compilers.\\n53: //\\n54: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n55: \\n56: #ifndef LLVM_TRANSFORMS_VECTORIZE_LOOPVECTORIZE_H\\n57: #define LLVM_TRANSFORMS_VECTORIZE_LOOPVECTORIZE_H\\n58: \\n59: #include \\\"llvm/IR/PassManager.h\\\"\\n60: #include \\\"llvm/Support/CommandLine.h\\\"\\n61: #include \\\"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\\\"\\n62: #include \\\"llvm/Transforms/Utils/ExtraPassManager.h\\\"\\n63: #include <functional>\\n64: \\n65: namespace llvm {\\n66: \\n67: class AssumptionCache;\\n68: class BlockFrequencyInfo;\\n69: class DemandedBits;\\n70: class DominatorTree;\\n71: class Function;\\n72: class Instruction;\\n73: class Loop;\\n74: class LoopAccessInfoManager;\\n75: class LoopInfo;\\n76: class OptimizationRemarkEmitter;\\n77: class ProfileSummaryInfo;\\n78: class ScalarEvolution;\\n79: class TargetLibraryInfo;\\n80: class TargetTransformInfo;\\n81: \\n82: LLVM_ABI extern cl::opt<bool> EnableLoopInterleaving;\\n83: LLVM_ABI extern cl::opt<bool> EnableLoopVectorization;\\n84: \\n85: struct LoopVectorizeOptions {\\n86:   /// If false, consider all loops for interleaving.\\n87:   /// If true, only loops that explicitly request interleaving are considered.\\n88:   bool InterleaveOnlyWhenForced;\\n89: \\n90:   /// If false, consider all loops for vectorization.\\n91:   /// If true, only loops that explicitly request vectorization are considered.\\n92:   bool VectorizeOnlyWhenForced;\\n93: \\n94:   /// The current defaults when creating the pass with no arguments are:\\n95:   /// EnableLoopInterleaving = true and EnableLoopVectorization = true. This\\n96:   /// means that interleaving default is consistent with the cl::opt flag, while\\n97:   /// vectorization is not.\\n98:   /// FIXME: The default for EnableLoopVectorization in the cl::opt should be\\n99:   /// set to true, and the corresponding change to account for this be made in\\n100:   /// opt.cpp. The initializations below will become:\\n101:   /// InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(!EnableLoopInterleaving)\\n102:   /// VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(!EnableLoopVectorization).\\n103:   LoopVectorizeOptions()\\n104:       : InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(false), VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(false) {}\\n105:   LoopVectorizeOptions(bool InterleaveOnlyWhenForced,\\n106:                        bool VectorizeOnlyWhenForced)\\n107:       : InterleaveOnlyWhenForced(InterleaveOnlyWhenForced),\\n108:         VectorizeOnlyWhenForced(VectorizeOnlyWhenForced) {}\\n109: \\n110:   LoopVectorizeOptions &setInterleaveOnlyWhenForced(bool Value) {\\n111:     InterleaveOnlyWhenForced = Value;\\n112:     return *this;\\n113:   }\\n114: \\n115:   LoopVectorizeOptions &setVectorizeOnlyWhenForced(bool Value) {\\n116:     VectorizeOnlyWhenForced = Value;\\n117:     return *this;\\n118:   }\\n119: };\\n120: \\n121: /// Storage for information about made changes.\\n122: struct LoopVectorizeResult {\\n123:   bool MadeAnyChange;\\n124:   bool It will\n55: /// initially scan the loop for existing metadata, and will update the local\n56: /// values based on information in the loop.\n57: /// We cannot write all values to metadata, as the mere presence of some info,\n58: /// for example 'force', means a decision has been made. So, we need to be\n59: /// careful NOT to add them if the user hasn't specifically asked so.\n60: class LoopVectorizeHints {\n61:   enum HintKind {\n62:     HK_WIDTH,\n63:     HK_INTERLEAVE,\n64:     HK_FORCE,\n65:     HK_ISVECTORIZED,\n66:     HK_PREDICATE,\n67:     HK_SCALABLE\n68:   };\n69: \n70:   /// Hint - associates name and validation with the hint value.\n71:   struct Hint {\n72:     const char *Name;\n73:     unsigned Value; // This may have to change for non-numeric values.\n74:     HintKind Kind;\n75: \n76:     Hint(const char *Name, unsigned Value, HintKind Kind)\n77:         : Name(Name), Value(Value), Kind(Kind) {}\n78: \n79:     bool validate(unsigned Val);\n80:   };\n81: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d@4152de6435984e9fc55431f4d74a7470d8ac05c0/-/blob/llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Vectorize/LoopVectorizationLegality.h%3FL1-80"}}}

//===- LoopVectorize.cpp - A Loop Vectorizer ------------------------------===//\n2: //\n3: // Part of the LLVM Project, under the Apache License v2.0 with LLVM Exceptions.\n4: // See https://llvm.org/LICENSE.txt for license information.\n5: // SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 WITH LLVM-exception\n6: //\n7: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n8: //\n9: // This is the LLVM loop vectorizer. This pass modifies 'vectorizable' loops\n10: // and generates target-independent LLVM-IR.\n11: // The vectorizer uses the TargetTransformInfo analysis to estimate the costs\n12: // of instructions in order to estimate the profitability of vectorization.\n13: //\n14: // The loop vectorizer combines consecutive loop iterations into a single\n15: // 'wide' iteration. After this transformation the index is incremented\n16: // by the SIMD vector width, and not by one.\n17: //\n18: // This pass has three parts:\n19: // 1. The main loop pass that drives the different parts.\n20: // 2. LoopVectorizationLegality - A unit that checks for the legality\n21: //    of the vectorization.\n22: // 3. InnerLoopVectorizer - A unit that performs the actual\n23: //    widening of instructions.\n24: // 4. LoopVectorizationCostModel - A unit that checks for the profitability\n25: //    of vectorization. It decides on the optimal vector width, which\n26: //    can be one, if vectorization is not profitable.\n27: //\n28: // There is a development effort going on to migrate loop vectorizer to the\n29: // VPlan infrastructure and to introduce outer loop vectorization support (see\n30: // docs/VectorizationPlan.rst and\n31: // http://lists.llvm.org/pipermail/llvm-dev/2017-December/119523.html). For this\n32: // purpose, we temporarily introduced the VPlan-native vectorization path: an\n33: // alternative vectorization path that is natively implemented on top of the\n34: // VPlan infrastructure. See EnableVPlanNativePath for enabling.\n35: //\n36: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n37: //\n38: // The reduction-variable vectorization is based on the paper:\n39: //  D. Nuzman and R. Henderson. Multi-platform Auto-vectorization.\n40: //\n41: // Variable uniformity checks are inspired by:\n42: //  Karrenberg, R. and Hack, S. Whole Function Vectorization.\n43: //\n44: // The interleaved access vectorization is based on the paper:\n45: //  Dorit Nuzman, Ira Rosen and Ayal Zaks.  Auto-Vectorization of Interleaved\n46: //  Data for SIMD\n47: //\n48: // Other ideas/concepts are from:\n49: //  A. Zaks and D. Nuzman. Autovectorization in GCC-two years later.\n50: //\n51: //  S. Maleki, Y. Gao, M. Garzaran, T. Wong and D. Padua.  An Evaluation of\n52: //  Vectorizing Compilers.\n53: //\n54: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n55: \n56: #include The pass accepts LoopVectorizeOptions to control behavior.\\n\\n2. **LoopVectorizeOptions** - A struct in `llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Vectorize/LoopVectorize.h` that controls pass behavior with two boolean flags: InterleaveOnlyWhenForced and VectorizeOnlyWhenForced.\\n\\n3. **LoopVectorizationLegality** - The legality checker that determines if a loop can be vectorized. Checks for memory dependencies, data flow, control flow legality, and induction/reduction variables.\\n\\n4. **LoopVectorizationCostModel** - The profitability analyzer defined directly in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Vectorize/LoopVectorize.cpp`. Determines profitable vectorization factors by estimating instruction costs using TargetTransformInfo and decides on the optimal vector width for the target architecture.\\n\\n5. **VPlan** - The Vectorization Plan data structure that represents the vectorized loop body before code generation. The class is defined in the private header `llvm/lib/Transforms/Vectorize/VPlan.h` with implementation in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Vectorize/VPlan.cpp`. VPlan provides a high-level representation of the vectorization strategy, allowing for cost estimation and optimization before generating final LLVM-IR code.\\n\\nThese five components work together: LoopVectorizePass orchestrates the process, LoopVectorizationLegality ensures correctness, LoopVectorizationCostModel selects profitable vector widths, and VPlan represents the intermediate vectorization plan that can be analyzed and optimized before code generation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1256,"cache_read_input_tokens":64631,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1256},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"78dabf95-e82c-4ad2-82ec-5cd3e2165d4e","uuid":"f8917ed4-5fff-4fa6-820a-b566aecddd79"}
